                  <hi rend="ital">The people,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">party, went forth going on foot; having no beasts:</hi> and the sing. is <foreign lang="ar">مِطْرَاقٌ</foreign>, (O,) or   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n26681-1" target="مُطْرِقٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n26676"/></foreign>, ('Eyn, L, * TA, *) accord. to A 'Obeyd; the latter, if correct, extr. (TA.)    </entryFree>3e:Tbb3,<entryFree id="n26682" key="مَطْرُوقٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">مَطْرُوقٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> [pass. part. n. of <foreign lang="ar">طَرَقَ</foreign>; <hi rend="ital">Beaten,</hi> &amp;c.]. <foreign lang="ar">هُوَ مَطْرُوقٌ</foreign> means <hi rend="ital">He is one whom every one beats</hi> or <hi rend="ital">slaps</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">يَطْرُقُهُ كُلُّ أَحَدٍ</foreign>). (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  And <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  A man <hi rend="ital">in whom is softness,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">flaccidity,</hi> (As, S, O, K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">and weakness:</hi> (As, S:) or <hi rend="ital">weakness and softness:</hi> (TA:) or <hi rend="ital">softness and flaccidity:</hi> from the saying <foreign lang="ar">هُوَ مَطْرُوقٌ</foreign> i. e. <foreign lang="ar">اصابته حادثة كتفته</foreign> [which, if we should read <foreign lang="ar">كَتَفَتْهُ</foreign>, seems to mean <hi rend="ital">he is smitten by an event,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">accident, that has</hi> disabled him as though it <hi rend="ital">bound his arms behind his back;</hi> but I think it probable that <foreign lang="ar">كتفته</foreign> is a mistranscription]: or because he is <foreign lang="ar">مصروف</foreign> [app. a mistake for <foreign lang="ar">مَضْرُوب</foreign>], like as one says <foreign lang="ar">مَقْرُوع</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَدَوَّخ</foreign> [app. meaning <hi rend="ital">beaten</hi> and <hi rend="ital">subdued,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">rendered submissive</hi>]: or as being likened, in abjectness, to a she-camel that is termed <foreign lang="ar">مَطْرُوقَةٌ</foreign> [like <foreign lang="ar">مَطَرَّقَةٌ</foreign> (q. v.)]. (Er-Rághib, TA.) <foreign lang="ar">مَطْرُوقَةٌ</foreign> applied to a woman means [app. <hi rend="ital">Soft and feminine;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">that does not make herself like a man.</hi> (TA.) [See also a reading of a verse cited voce <foreign lang="ar">مَطْرُوفٌ</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Also <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">Weak in intellect,</hi> (K, TA,) <hi rend="ital">and soft.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  Applied to herbage, <hi rend="ital">Smitten by the rain after its having dried up.</hi> (Ibn-'Abbád, L, K.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">طَرْقٌ</foreign>, latter half. Applied to a ewe, <foreign lang="ar">مَطْرُوقَةٌ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">Branded with the mark called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">طِرَاق</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">upon the middle of her ear.</hi> (ISh, O, K.)
